          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2554837610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15288006073256357045">"Demon from the Dark" is the 9:th book in Kresley Cole`s paranormal "Immortals After Dark"-series that satisfied and enthranced me with its hardcore action,sensual and charming romance with two awesome characters that stole my heart.This book have EVERYTHING i love in a paranormal romance,it was a different read but highly addictive.I atet up every word of it and i can`t wait for the next one.<br/><br/>Along with other immortals the beautiful witch Carrow Graie gets captured by the mortals who hates their</span>
  <span id="freeText15288006073256357045" style="display:none">"Demon from the Dark" is the 9:th book in Kresley Cole`s paranormal "Immortals After Dark"-series that satisfied and enthranced me with its hardcore action,sensual and charming romance with two awesome characters that stole my heart.This book have EVERYTHING i love in a paranormal romance,it was a different read but highly addictive.I atet up every word of it and i can`t wait for the next one.<br /><br />Along with other immortals the beautiful witch Carrow Graie gets captured by the mortals who hates their kind.They blackmail her in forcing her to lure Malkolm Slaine into their clutches and in turn they will give her and her newly orphaned niece Ruby freedom.She never expected that man to be her fated mate when she meets him.<br /><br />Carrow Graie is a very badass witch that gets empowered by others emotions.She is a very sensual creature that takes on Ruby as her daughter and is willing to do everything to save her-even betray her fated mate.She was so torn and heartbroken over what she had to do that i deeply felt sorry for her and i wished that she somehow could find a way to undo it.But i love how she accepted and loved him for the man he is with scars and all,it made for a beautiful love-story!<br /><br />Malkom Slaine is the feared Scarba-a half vampire and demon.He is one of the most tortured heroes of KC`s.What he went through as a child to those vampire fuckers made me want to throw up.Everyone betrayed him in a way or other,no wonder he lived isolated and alone for so many centuries.Despite his dark,rugged and dangerous appearance..there was so much innocence in him.(It makes it even better that he was a virgin)He worshipped the ground Carrow walked on and her joy was his.I nearly cried for his blind love for her,since the last thing he expected was that she would betray him.His and Carrow`s love for each other was deep,sweet,raw,sexy and eternal.Point end,they belong with each other.I also loved how he saw Ruby as his daughter,the ending was so bittersweet!<br /><br />I have known that Declan Chase is the incarnation of Aidan the Fierce,the fated mate of valkyrie Regin and that he dies everytime he remembers his past memories of loving Regin.But this side of Declan is so vicious and dark that i was shit scared of him!He also tortures Regin more than the others and i am so afraid of the next book since i know it will be their story.But damn,i am so EXCITED!We also get cameo appearences by Conrad and Neomi and that made me jump with happiness since i love this couple to the death!I also wondered where the hell Nix is in this book when everybody needed her!But she makes me laugh and for that i love her.This book is another 5-star for me,it was perfect,angsty,romantic,funny and so sweet and steamy.I LOVED IT!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15288006073256357045" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1008173487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4536697250355205001">I return for more dramas on the 'Island Of Immortals, Monsters and Evil Humans'!<br/><br/>This time the book takes us to the nameless Island where the evil Order kept the immortals and monsters of the Lore prisoners and did evil experiments on them. Carrow, a young fun-loving witch is among the prisoners, when the Order blackmailed Carrow with the life of her seven years old cousin, she had to agree to go to a terrifying hell plane to lurk a powerful demon and capture him so the Order could do evil experi</span>
  <span id="freeText4536697250355205001" style="display:none">I return for more dramas on the 'Island Of Immortals, Monsters and Evil Humans'!<br><br>This time the book takes us to the nameless Island where the evil Order kept the immortals and monsters of the Lore prisoners and did evil experiments on them. Carrow, a young fun-loving witch is among the prisoners, when the Order blackmailed Carrow with the life of her seven years old cousin, she had to agree to go to a terrifying hell plane to lurk a powerful demon and capture him so the Order could do evil experiments on this rare hybrid between demon and vampire...<br><br>To be honest, I think the ending of this volume of Immortals After Dark is a bit on the weak side, still I enjoy the development of both the male and female leads and the interactions between them are rather sweet as well.<br><br>The male lead is one of the closest thing to a 'caveman' I've seen among the paranormal romances. Let's see, the guy is from an isolated 'master-slave' demonic society and he had been tortured and betrayed for most of his long, lone life. It does help to explain some of his behaviors. Not that I'm 100% okay with it (for a few times I even worried that he is getting close to force himself on the girl but luckily he doesn't) but I can understand where he came from, I think this time Ms. Cole didn't overdo her tortured male lead too much--I mean, it also helps that the guy hadn't spoken much in the story and he hadn't said or done thing which makes me dislike him.<br><br>Our heroine, Carrow is such a sweetheart! She has a colorful personality and she is a streetwise, sassy girl who you can relate with, the interactions among her, her little cousin and her female friends are also sweet. <br><br>As to the love scenes/smuts in the story, what can I say? I don't love it, but I do think they are pretty hot...<br><br>Like this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456152266i/18196807.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.pinterest.com/phyllisjustice9/mejibray/">https://www.pinterest.com/phyllisjust...</a>)<br><br>I still want to read more from this series.<br><br>PS: I'm really loving The Queen of Gold and Evil and the mayhem she brings at her wake~<br><br>PSS: My drawing which is inspired by this novel:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484316932i/21708050._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://vampirekiki.deviantart.com/art/drawing-inspired-by-Kresley-Cole-s-novels-586796991">http://vampirekiki.deviantart.com/art...</a>)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9567254271475953814">4.5 stars<br/><br/>LOVED LOVED LOVED this!! So glad i ended my 2016 book challenge with this fantastic paranormal read. What a way to end my year! <br/><br/>Carrow, a beautiful, sassy witch has to lure Malkom, a 400 year old vemon(vampire-demon) to a designated place and in that time she begins to love this grossly misunderstood, bad-tempered male.   <span id="freeText9567254271475953814" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />LOVED LOVED LOVED this!! So glad i ended my 2016 book challenge with this fantastic paranormal read. What a way to end my year! <br /><br />Carrow, a beautiful, sassy witch has to lure Malkom, a 400 year old vemon(vampire-demon) to a designated place and in that time she begins to love this grossly misunderstood, bad-tempered male. What starts off as a mutual attraction and understanding ends with the utmost betrayal and Carrow has to find her way to burrow back into Malkolm's heart. I LOVED this demon. Despite him trying so hard to hang on to his hate, he was still so protective of Carrow and i especially loved his relationship with Ruby. <br /><br />Lotsa angst, action and grovelling from the heroine, out of this world sexy times and an amazing relationship between the main characters.... I definitely recommend this book to PNR fans. This was a complete standalone, although characters from other books make an appearance. I did not feel lost and caught up pretty easily. Will definitely catch up with the rest in this series in 2017. <br /><br />HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!</span>

<div id="review_265406137" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/265406137" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/265406137?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781849830379" href="/book/show/7933795-demon-from-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=vampire-shapeshifters">vampire-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer265406137" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13950061946817916356">I love the world that Kresley Cole has created in her Immortals After Dark Series. The world of Lore filled with fey, werewolves, ghosts, demons, women strong, tortured and violent as the men with witty, pop culture dialogue…and incredibly hot smoking steaming scenes. She takes us through vivid journeys that even though your sane brain tells you…no not possible….the impossible become possible!!!!<br/> Demon from the Dark is one of the most touching and poignant stories I have read in the series so fa</span>
  <span id="freeText13950061946817916356" style="display:none">I love the world that Kresley Cole has created in her Immortals After Dark Series. The world of Lore filled with fey, werewolves, ghosts, demons, women strong, tortured and violent as the men with witty, pop culture dialogue…and incredibly hot smoking steaming scenes. She takes us through vivid journeys that even though your sane brain tells you…no not possible….the impossible become possible!!!!<br /> Demon from the Dark is one of the most touching and poignant stories I have read in the series so far. <br />The Order, a group of evil and cruel humans, whose aim is to destroy and kill all immortals, has kidnapped Carrow Graie, a witch who hides her pain and sorrow behind a party-animal life is forced to cross to another realm and bring back Malkom Slaine, a ruthless half-demon, half-vampire or they will kill someone close to her.<br /><br />Malkom is such a tormented, lonely alpha hero. As a small child, his prostitute mother had sold him as a blood slave to a vampire, where he was abused and tortured repeatedly and after escaping, became a warrior fighting vampires. After all the betrayals, torture and forced to kill his best friend, he flees to a desert wasteland, where he has lived in isolation for thousands of years, forgetting how to speak and trying to keep alive to continue his vengeance against those you want him dead. On the verge of losing his sanity he discovers a beautiful, green-eyed woman that touches his heart and he realizes she is his mate and will never let her go. He will give his life for hers.<br />Carrow is at first terrified of this dirty looking, huge monster but after he takes her to his cave home, where he shows her such tenderness and kindness, her feelings begin to change.<br /><br />Both feel something deep and profound for each other. Their chemistry is unmistakable. I loved the scenes where he watches her bathing in an amazing rock pool deep in the cave….wow…it’s a pretty steamy scene. And when she cuts his hair and washes him, so touching…I could almost feel Malkom’s wonder and what he was feeling….such a long time since anyone had touched him, shown him any tenderness. <br />The build-up to Carrow and Malkom escaping the realm was taut, nail-biting.<br /><br />Malkom is one of my favorite heroes….honorable, passionate, caring and loving and nothing means more to him than protecting Carrow and her niece Ruby…he will do anything for them, even dying for them.<br /><br />Such extraordinary characters…..love the way the author gets us to meet up again with characters from previous books and meeting new ones that will lead to their own books.<br /><br />Please do yourself a favor…….READ THIS BOOK. It will touch your heart!!!!<br /><br />Kresley Cole, you are amazing and I thank you for sharing this world with me…….<br /><br /><br />Here’s the brief synopsis<br />A scorching tale of a demon outcast poisoned with vampire blood and the vulnerable young witch he vows to protect—even from himself.<br />A dangerous demon she can’t resist<br />Malkom Slaine: Tormented by his sordid past and racked by vampiric hungers, he’s pushed to the brink by the green-eyed beauty under his guard.<br />A maddening witch he aches to claim<br />Carrow Graie: Hiding her own sorrows, she lives only for the next party or prank. Until she meets a tortured warrior worth saving.<br />Trapped together in a savage prison<br />For them to survive, Malkom must unleash both the demon and vampire inside him. When he becomes the nightmare his own people feared, will he lose the woman he craves body and soul?<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13950061946817916356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

On to Regan and Aiden! Happy reading!<br/><br/><b>Original Review May 28, 2013</b><br/><br/>My favorite IAD book so far! Malkolm has become my favorite IAD male. So sweet and vulnerable yet barbaric and fierce. He reminds me of Zadist from the BDB series or even Zane</span>
  <span id="freeText16865939908097153504" style="display:none"><b>Reread Review September 24, 2017</b><br /><br />5+ "Barbarian Vemon" Stars!<br /><br />LOVED, LOVED, LOVED!!! I am so happy I still love theses stories. I still absolutely adore Malcolm. So broken, so fierce, so protective, so swoony. Le sigh. I'm enjoying rereading this series so much. On to Regan and Aiden! Happy reading!<br /><br /><b>Original Review May 28, 2013</b><br /><br />My favorite IAD book so far! Malkolm has become my favorite IAD male. So sweet and vulnerable yet barbaric and fierce. He reminds me of Zadist from the BDB series or even Zane from the Scanguard Vampire series, both of whom I love. Clearly I like the redeemed tortured survivor type. I usually am a wolf girl but Malkolm made me fall for a vemon! Carrow is a good character too. She is not one to sit around waiting to be rescued, maybe even doing a little rescuing her self... I believe in their HEA. I highly recommend this one. Now I'm on to the next book. Regan and Aiden's story... how is THAT going to work out? We'll see. Happy reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16865939908097153504" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_77802819" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/77802819" />
    <a title="Jill Myles" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2368931-jill-myles"><img alt="Jill Myles" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442500872p2/2368931.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/77802819?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill Myles" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill Myles" href="/user/show/2368931-jill-myles">Jill Myles</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2368931-jill-myles?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer77802819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16927466154380859371">ETA - Re-read! Drank this down in an afternoon. Loved it, though I wish Carrow and Malkom could have had more 'alone' time. ;)<br/><br/><br/>Kresley Cole is one of my favorite authors today. So far she has not hit a sour note for me. So it's no surprise to me that I loved this book, but it did surprise me how MUCH I loved it.<br/><br/>I should start by saying that the House of Witches aren't my favorite Loreans. I get a little miffed every time there's a non-valkyrie heroine. So my excitement for this book? Not nearly a</span>
  <span id="freeText16927466154380859371" style="display:none">ETA - Re-read! Drank this down in an afternoon. Loved it, though I wish Carrow and Malkom could have had more 'alone' time. ;)<br /><br /><br />Kresley Cole is one of my favorite authors today. So far she has not hit a sour note for me. So it's no surprise to me that I loved this book, but it did surprise me how MUCH I loved it.<br /><br />I should start by saying that the House of Witches aren't my favorite Loreans. I get a little miffed every time there's a non-valkyrie heroine. So my excitement for this book? Not nearly as much as it was for Regin's (which is coming in February). However, Kresley Cole proved me totally wrong - this book totally brought its A-Game and it's easily one of the best in the series.<br /><br />Why is it one of the best? Three words for you: Malkom, Malkom, Malkom. Who would have thought that a vemon would be so sexy or so tortured? Kresley's never shied away from putting her characters in tough positions, and this book is no different. Malkom grew up a tortured slave boy to sadistic vampires and that was probably the high point of his existence. He's turned into a vampire (vemon = vampire demon) and then hunted by the other demons in his plane. He's never touched a woman, never had anyone look at him with affection or want or love. He's gone wild in the centuries that he's been hunted, covered in dirt and filth, hated by all...<br /><br />And then pretty Carrow shows up and his heart starts beating. I WAS TOTALLY IN LOVE. From this point on, Malkom is the beast trying to get 'beauty' to give her heart to him, and it was A M A Z I N G. /fangirl<br /><br />Soooo good. I closed it and immediately wanted to start reading it again. That's when you know it's an awesome read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16927466154380859371" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5lUpw9z+Ikgwj+BofusKJv8NleiY3f2jcIQ+ZhrTiDrcc0ARZ6DrIJekVAmJHgD5KVJyIFZQc8Qr+njX15B6oA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1QFSmnro37wmSQJs2Z1HgbWLs8dkl036+S6hbYRazaTvJztIwbYW1IFitg0uaE1eY9RUD6oaw52iUOfcSRk/Pg==')})
  }
